          Biden announces the US will have enough vaccines for 'every adult in America' by the end of May
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="tout-copy featured-tout typography">
         <ul>
          <li>
           This comes after the US Food and Drug Administration authorized Johnson &amp; Johnson's COVID-19 vaccine for emergency use over the weekend.
          </li>
          <li>
           Biden announced that Merck will work with Johnson &amp; Johnson to manufacture the new vaccine.
          </li>
          <li>
           The president said he hopes "by this time next year, we're going to be back to normal." But he called on Americans to "continue to be smart" about following COVID-19 mitigation guidelines.
          </li>
         </ul>
